<p>From, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ะฐะฟััฃะปั</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aprฤlฤญ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, earlier <span class="Cyrs" lang="orv">ะฐะฟัะธะปั</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="tr Latn">aprilฤญ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ฮฯฯฮฏฮปฮนฮฟฯ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Aprรญlios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Aprฤซlis</i> from (perhaps) Etruscan <i class="Ital mention" lang="ett">๐๐๐๐</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ett-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apru</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">แผฯฯฮฟฮดฮฏฯฮท</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Aphrodรญtฤ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Grammatically the word is a masculine, but it is used to refer to both a man and a woman and it is declinable in both cases. The term <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ะฐะฟัะตฬะบะฐััะฐ</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">aptรฉkarลกa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is also used for a woman in colloquial Russian.</li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐัะตะฝะฐ.html>ะฐัะตฬะฝะฐ</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">arรฉna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐัะตะฝะฐ.html>ะฐัะตฬะฝั</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐัะตะฝะฐ.html>ะฐัะตฬะฝั</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐัะตะฝะฐ.html>ะฐัะตฬะฝ</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐัะตััะฐะฝั.html>ะฐัะตััะฐฬะฝั</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arestรกnt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ัะบะธะน</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐัะตััะฐะฝััะบะธะน.html>ะฐัะตััะฐฬะฝััะบะธะน</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">arestรกntskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
